<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sores.html>sores</a> (22418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">צרות</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsores</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">צרה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsore</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouble.html>trouble</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:problem.html>problem</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">צָרָה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsará</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouble.html>trouble</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedy.html>tragedy</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:calamity.html>calamity</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sores.html>sores</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number"><a href = vnd.unilang:pl.html>pl</a></abbr></span> (<i>plural <a href = vnd.unilang:only.html>only</a></i>)

<ol><li>tsuris; <a href = vnd.unilang:misery.html>misery</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:worry.html>worry</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sous.html>sous</a> (88028)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:saus.html>saus</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:sous.html>sous</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af p-form-of" lang="af">souse</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af diminutive-form-of" lang="af">sousie</b>)
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sowieso.html>sowieso</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> negated <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sowieso.html>sowieso</a></i> (“not necessarily”) <a href = vnd.unilang:does.html>does</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:exist.html>exist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> uses <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unbedingt</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:instead.html>instead</a>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spaarzaam.html>spaarzaam</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">spaarzaamer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">spaarzaamst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sparing, frugal, <a href = vnd.unilang:thrifty.html>thrifty</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spanjool.html>spanjool</a> (40158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">español</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanjool.html>spanjool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanjolen.html>spanjolen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanjool.html>spanjooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
